The "Greater China Treasure Hunt" package pre-sold by Ctrip can be said to be cost-effective. Since the last time he was accidentally promoted to a "Greater China Treasure Hunt" theme room in a hotel in Shanghai, his son has been obsessed with it. This themed room this time is a small suite with a separate living room area and enough space for free extra beds. There is no pressure for a family of three. However, the hotel itself has been completed and renovated for many years, and it is a bit outdated. For example, the washbasin is an old fashion, which is easy to splash and is not very practical to use. The overall area of the room is limited. The big bed is a mini size, and it is not as wide as the big bed at home. It can be considered as an increase in intimacy. There was a tent for children to play in the room. A child got up early in the morning and went in and spent an hour alone (to read the "Great Shanghai Treasure Hunt" provided in the room).
Both check-in and check-out are actually peak hours. However, there is a situation where there is only one person at the front desk, and the waiting time is relatively long. But when checking-in, I met a very professional and empathetic receptionist, so that the degree of goodwill for the hotel skyrocketed. (At the same time, it did increase the strange knowledge) However, what I encountered when checking out was not negligence, and perhaps a more normal reception attitude, which inevitably makes people feel "inexpensive and old". The service is from the original high-end hotel. Gradually on a downward slope, the standards stemming from management are no longer what they used to be.

The breakfast variety is not too small, but the taste is mediocre. The local selection of yogurt is bright, and the handwork is well received.
Generally speaking, if the price is less than 1,000 yuan, the price/performance ratio is good. In the morning, you can walk to Hongqiao Greenbelt in 5 minutes. The World Trade Center next door has trampoline/fencing and other sports venues, all within walking distance.
The suite parking is free, which is another point worthy of manual praise.
BTW, the swimming pool area is very very very very limited, which is about ten grades behind the standard swimming pool. But the advantage is that because the venue is too limited, there is basically no one. After dinner, the venue will be booked and equipped with a luxurious lineup of two lifeguards.
